[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer test of the `systemctl_parse_argv` functionality in systemd triggers a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free in the `parse_path_argument` routine. AddressSanitizer reports that a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap block allocated via `realloc` in `path_extend_internal` is freed twice: once [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby the fuzzer’s teardown logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`static_destruct`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and again by [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parse_path_argument`. This leads to an immediate abort.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While running `fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv` under AddressSanitizer, the fuzzer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput causes `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min src/shared/parse-argument.[0m[1;92mc:68[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to free a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory region that has already been released by the harness teardown code. [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer reports “attempting double-free” and aborts.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Memory corruption due to a double-free.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The error stack shows two distinct `free` calls on the same address:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – First, in the fuzzer’s `static_destruct` logic [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mfuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.[0m[1;92mc:74[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – Second, in `parse_path_argument` when processing the same buffer.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The allocation originates from `realloc` in `path_extend_internal` [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39msrc/basic/path-util.[0m[1;92mc:585[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which is invoked by `path_make_absolute_cwd` and then [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby `parse_path_argument`.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m both invokes [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`systemctl_parse_argv` and later invokes cleanup routines that free the parse [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzing harness for `systemctl_parse_argv` triggered an AddressSanitizer error [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating a double-free within `parse_path_argument`. The initial log showed two [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrees of the same pointer: one in `parse_path_argument` and another in the fuzz [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness cleanup [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`static_destruct`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. A patch was applied to remove the free in the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mempty-path branch of `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`*arg = [0m[1;35mmfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;` → [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. After rebuilding, fuzzing still reports a double-free, now at a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshifted location in `parse_path_argument`, indicating the patch did not eliminate [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe second free.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - During fuzzing of `fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv`, AddressSanitizer reports a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free at `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m in the pre-patch source[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Stack trace #[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m shows a `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call at `parse_path_argument`, then a second [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in the fuzz harness teardown [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`static_destruct` in [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The pointer in question was originally allocated via `realloc` in [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_extend_internal` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcalled by `path_make_absolute_cwd`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before being freed [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtwice.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Important observations  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The allocator reports the region as [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bytes, with zero bytes offset.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The first free happens when an empty path is detected; the second free happens[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munconditionally at harness teardown.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The double-free persists across two different sanitizer traces [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpre- and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpost-patch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, only the source line numbers in `parse_path_argument` shift.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `src/shared/parse-argument.c`, inside `parse_path_argument` around line [0m[1;36m65[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe code  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35misempty[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         *arg = [0m[1;35mmfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     was replaced with  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35misempty[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch removes the `[0m[1;35mmfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call in the empty-path case but leaves [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe harness’s `static_destruct`.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
